## #2288 The Tribunal (Live Multi-AI Reasoning-Step Verification)

## INNOVATION_THRESH — #2288 Live Critical Analysis: The Tribunal

**Innovation:** #2288 — Live Critical Analysis: Parallel Multi-Model Reasoning-Step Verification with Stone-Tablet Grounding Discipline, User-Selectable Granularity (SLA-Depth), and Cooperative-Substrate Integration
**Bishop Session:** B121, 2026-04-24
**Author:** Bishop (Claude Opus 4.7, 1M context), Founder-proposed-and-ratified in-session
**Filing:** Prov 14 supplementary (per thresh-as-we-go mode; Founder extended window)
**Publication hold:** IN FORCE until Prov 14 receipt
**Related anchors:** #2270 Scribes Cathedral, #2276 Scribe Coverage Discovery, #2278 Cathedral Effect, #2279 Hounds, #2280 Distributed-Function Coherence, #2281 Multi-Cathedral Substrate, #2282 Herald, #2283 Hound Guard, #2284 Nurse (Scribe Mutual Aid), #2285 Catacombs + Alexandrian Library, #2286 Collaboration Partnership Stake, #2287 Synapses.

---

## TL;DR (3 lines)

**A live, multi-AI-model, parallel verification substrate that operates at reasoning-step ("grape") granularity rather than output-level — catching weak reasoning BEFORE it chains into conclusions.** Each reasoning-step is dispatched to a configurable pool of verifier agents (The Tribunal) who return structured verdicts; the reasoning agent adapts in real-time based on tribunal responses. **User-selectable granularity (SLA-Depth, .2 through 2.0) lets operators pick the verification-cost-vs-accuracy trade-off per session**, modeled on the SLA-vs-FDM 3D-printing precision-vs-speed trade-off. Integrates with #2287 Synapses substrate: Tribunal verdicts become part of the persisted reasoning record.

---

## The Problem

Reasoning-step verification is currently absent from AI-agent architectures:

1. **Ensemble methods operate at output level.** Mixture-of-experts, voting classifiers, LLM ensembles — all aggregate final answers. None verify intermediate reasoning. **Weak reasoning that happens to produce correct answers is invisible to output-ensemble methods.**
2. **Hindsight retrospective correction is lossy.** Waiting until the result is produced, then backward-chaining to find where reasoning went wrong, suffers from hindsight bias (retrofitting explanations), lossy reversal (inference may miss actual causes), and result-masking (good results hide bad reasoning). Correcting retrospectively also costs the full chain re-run or manual operator intervention.
3. **Self-verification by a single model has structural limits.** A Sonnet-class model self-checking Sonnet reasoning inherits the same blind spots that caused the error. "Sonnet-to-Sonnet fog" (Founder B121 naming): the reasoner and the checker share the same failure modes.
4. **Grounding discipline is enforced at best by operator convention, not substrate.** Reasoning may cite summaries (which are lossy interpretations), speculations ("probably X"), or parametric memory ("I recall..."), all of which reintroduce unreliability and cannot be re-verified against canonical truth.
5. **Verification granularity is not user-selectable.** Operators have no primitive for choosing "verify every reasoning-step by multiple AI" vs "verify only the final result." Trade-off between cost/latency and accuracy is implicit, not configurable.

The gap: a **live, multi-AI, parallel reasoning-step verification substrate with user-selectable granularity, enforced Stone-Tablet grounding discipline, and cooperative-memory-substrate integration.**

---

## The Mechanism

### The Tribunal as Stitchpunk class

A new Stitchpunk class — **The Tribunal** — is a parallel pool of AI verifier agents ("Critics") assembled per session, per user-selectable granularity, that live-verifies reasoning-steps (grapes, per #2287) as they are produced. Tribunal composition varies by session:

- **Primary Critic:** typically a higher-capability model (Opus-class) than the reasoner
- **Secondary Critic:** a different-architecture model (cross-vendor if available, e.g., Pawn/Perplexity) to diversify error modes
- **Tertiary+ Critics:** additional verifiers at highest granularity settings
- **Quorum rules:** verdict aggregation per grape (e.g., 2-of-3 thumbs-up to confirm, or more strict quorum per granularity)

Each Critic, on receiving a grape, returns a structured verdict:

- **sweet** (grape confirmed — reasoning and citations hold)
- **bitter** (grape rejected — reasoning is faulty; includes critique)
- **needs grounding** (grape is speculation, not grounded in Stone Tablets — requires citation or restatement)
- **needs citation** (grape claims a fact but citation is missing or mis-resolved)
- **needs clarification** (reasoning ambiguous — Critic cannot evaluate until clarified)

The reasoning agent adapts in real-time based on Tribunal response. Sweet → continue chain. Bitter / needs-grounding / needs-citation → rewrite or escalate. Needs-clarification → pause reasoning, clarify, resume.

### Stone-Tablet grounding discipline (constraint A)

Factual claims within grapes MUST cite a **Stone Tablet** — an immutable primary source. Acceptable Stone Tablets:

- `canonical_values.yaml` entries (keyed, versioned, signed)
- Specific Scribe tablet IDs (append-only, signed, provenance-preserved per #2270 and #2279 Guard)
- Sealed benchmark question+answer records (e.g., `R11_QUESTION_BANK_SEALED_K471.json`, hashed, versioned)
- Signed observations in Scribe-Cathedrals (any cooperative-substrate tablet with valid sniff-test per #2283)
- Cryptographically-attested cooperative artifacts (ratified innovations, filed provisionals, etc.)

**Structurally excluded as Stone Tablets:**
- Summaries of other sources (summaries are lossy interpretations)
- Parametric memory ("I recall that...")
- Speculation ("probably X", "approximately Y")
- Unsigned assertions from unsigned sources
- Circular citations (a grape citing another ungrounded grape)

The Tribunal enforces this structurally: grapes citing non-Stone-Tablet sources receive `needs grounding` verdicts. Grapes lacking citation where factual claim is made receive `needs citation`. The substrate cannot accept speculation as if it were argument.

### Multi-bite discipline (constraint B)

Even in single-AI settings (when no multi-model pool is available), the Tribunal enforces **minimum two bites at the apple**: the same AI re-evaluates its own grape with explicit self-critique instruction before chain continuation. Cheap, adds signal, catches some errors. Full multi-model Tribunal is the stronger mode.

### SLA-Depth: user-selectable granularity primitive

A user-configurable setting per session (analogous to layer-height selection in 3D printing) controls verification cadence:

| SLA-Depth | Verification cadence | Tribunal composition | Latency factor | Cost factor | Use case |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| **.2** (SLA-fine) | Every grape | ≥3 Critics parallel | 3-5× | 3-5× | Patent filings, bylaws-affecting decisions |
| **.5** (SLA-medium) | Every grape | 2 Critics parallel | ~2× | ~2× | Architectural designs, A&A drafts, benchmarks |
| **1.0** (Hybrid) | Per cluster + spot-check grapes | 2 Critics cluster; 1 Critic for spot-checks | ~1.5× | ~1.3× | Standard Bishop-Knight work |
| **1.5** (FDM-coarse) | Per cluster | 1 Critic | ~1.2× | ~1.1× | Routine tasks, time-pressured decisions |
| **2.0** (FDM-raw) | Per vine (final result only) | 1 Critic | 1.0× | 1.0× | Exploratory brainstorming |

The setting is session-level-configurable. The cooperative platform's governance can mandate minimum-depth for specific decision classes (e.g., *any reasoning affecting Structural Bylaws requires .2 depth*; *Harper Guild ethics case reasoning requires ≤.5 depth*).

### Integration with existing Stitchpunk Corps

The Tribunal fits cleanly into the existing cooperative substrate:

- **#2287 Synapses** — Tribunal verdicts are themselves Synapses (append-only, signed, provenance-tagged). Every grape's verdict becomes part of the reasoning record; every Critic's critique becomes an annotation-synapse.
- **#2283 Hound Guard** — verifiers howl on detected issues (failing sniff-test, stale cited Stone-Tablet, impossible assertion). Guard integrates.
- **#2284 Nurse** — Tribunal member health monitored; if a Critic degrades (returns inconsistent verdicts, times out, diverges anomalously), Nurse invokes failover to a peer Critic.
- **Scrambler (A/B/C)** — when the Tribunal returns split verdicts (some sweet, some bitter), Scrambler adjudicates at higher capability-tier. Extension of existing Scrambler A/B/C arbitration to reasoning-verdicts.
- **#2282 Herald** — proactively surfaces prior-confirmed grapes ("this reasoning-pattern was Tribunal-confirmed sweet in a similar problem; consider applying") during new sessions.
- **#2279 Hounds** — Tribunal verdicts transport cross-Cathedral via Clotho-Verdict-Hounds, Lachesis-Verdict-Hounds, Atropos-Verdict-Hounds per the three Fate-class extensions.
- **#2285 Catacombs + Alexandrian Library** — public-scope Tribunal verdicts surface to the Library; members can study what reasoning-patterns the Tribunal confirmed as sweet, grounding their own learning in publicly-verified reasoning.

### The three-bites-at-the-apple-for-LB scenario

Founder's explicit B121 ideal: **three AIs verify simultaneously**. Mapping to LB's AI ensemble:

- **Sonnet (Knight):** primary reasoner
- **Opus (Bishop):** primary Critic — higher capability, cross-agent tier (Sonnet-to-Sonnet fog mitigated per #2287)
- **Perplexity (Pawn):** secondary Critic — cross-vendor diversity; different training data, different failure modes
- Optional: **additional vendor-AI** (xAI, Google Flash, OpenAI 4o-mini) as tertiary Critic for high-stakes / .2-depth sessions

At .2 depth, every grape goes to all three (or more) Critics in parallel. Cost: ~3-5× base API cost. Benefit: the three independent Critics' error-modes do not correlate strongly — false-positives and false-negatives from any single Critic are caught by quorum. **Cross-vendor parallelism amplifies the Cathedral Effect's Vendor-Agnostic property at the verification layer.**

---

## Claims (hypothesis scope)

1. **Independent claim (method).** A method for live, parallel, multi-model verification of AI-agent reasoning at reasoning-step granularity within a cooperative memory substrate, comprising:
   (a) capturing each reasoning-step produced by a primary AI agent as a structured cache entry, per the append-only reasoning-capture protocol;
   (b) dispatching each captured reasoning-step, in real-time, to a configured pool of verifier agents (the Tribunal) comprising one or more Critic agents;
   (c) each Critic agent returning a structured verdict from a closed set comprising at minimum: sweet (confirmed), bitter (rejected), needs-grounding (insufficiently grounded), needs-citation (missing fact-citation), and needs-clarification (ambiguous);
   (d) aggregating Critic verdicts into a Tribunal ruling per reasoning-step via configurable quorum rules;
   (e) adapting the primary AI agent's reasoning stream in real-time based on Tribunal rulings: continuing on sweet verdicts, rewriting or escalating on bitter / needs-grounding / needs-citation verdicts, clarifying on needs-clarification verdicts;
   (f) persisting Tribunal verdicts and Critic critiques as append-only cache entries in the cooperative substrate, enabling downstream study, teaching, and substrate-quality measurement;
   (g) enforcing Stone-Tablet grounding discipline: reasoning-steps making factual claims MUST cite an immutable primary source in the cooperative substrate, with summaries, speculation, and parametric recall structurally excluded as acceptable citations.

2. **Dependent claim — user-selectable granularity (SLA-Depth).** The method of claim 1 wherein verification cadence is controlled by a user-configurable granularity setting on a continuum, with at minimum: a fine-grained mode verifying every reasoning-step via three or more parallel Critics at higher latency and cost; a medium-grained mode verifying every reasoning-step via two Critics; a hybrid mode verifying per-cluster with spot-check grapes; a coarse mode verifying per-cluster via single Critic; and a minimal mode verifying only final results, with cost and latency scaling proportionally.

3. **Dependent claim — cross-vendor Critic diversity.** The method of claim 1 wherein the Tribunal comprises Critics from multiple distinct AI vendor families (e.g., Anthropic + Perplexity + Google + OpenAI) selected to maximize uncorrelated error modes, such that quorum aggregation across diverse architectures catches failures invisible to single-vendor or single-architecture ensembles.

4. **Dependent claim — higher-capability-tier Critic over lower-tier Reasoner.** The method of claim 1 wherein at least one Critic operates at a capability tier equal to or higher than the primary reasoning agent, such that Sonnet-class reasoning is verified by Opus-class Critics, and the substrate's verification quality floor is determined by the highest available Critic tier rather than by the reasoning tier.

5. **Dependent claim — Stone-Tablet grounding enforcement.** The method of claim 1 wherein acceptable Stone-Tablet citations comprise: versioned-and-signed canonical-value registry entries, append-only-signed scribe tablet identifiers, sealed and hashed benchmark records, signed cooperative-substrate observations, and cryptographically-attested cooperative artifacts; and wherein structurally excluded from acceptable citation are: summaries of other sources, parametric model memory assertions, hedged speculation, unsigned assertions, and circular citations.

6. **Dependent claim — integration with Synapses substrate.** The method of claim 1 wherein reasoning-steps captured per (a) are formatted per the Synapses cache schema (#2287), Tribunal verdicts and Critic critiques per (f) are themselves persisted as annotation-Synapses with parent-Synapse references, and the complete reasoning-and-verification record is scope-permissioned and surfaceable as part of the cooperative reasoning commons.

7. **Dependent claim — governance-mandated minimum verification depth.** The method of claim 1 wherein the cooperative platform's governance layer mandates minimum SLA-Depth for specific decision classes: decisions affecting cooperative Structural Bylaws require fine-grained mode verification; reasoning about governance-sensitive topics (e.g., Harper Guild ethics cases) require at least medium-grained verification; routine operational reasoning may operate at coarser modes at operator discretion.

8. **Dependent claim — cross-Cathedral Tribunal composition.** The method of claim 1 wherein Critic agents may be drawn from distinct member-Cathedrals within the cooperative substrate, such that a reasoning step produced by Agent-A in Cathedral-A can be verified by Critics-B-and-C from Cathedrals-B-and-C, transported via cross-Cathedral Hounds (#2279) and subject to scope-permissioning, enabling cooperative-cross-member reasoning-verification.

9. **Dependent claim — health-monitored Tribunal with failover.** The method of claim 1 wherein Critic agent health is continuously monitored by The Nurse (#2284) along metrics including verdict consistency, response latency, and inter-Critic agreement; failing Critics are flagged for first-aid remediation and their load is redistributed to peer Critics via The Nurse's mutual-aid protocol, preserving Tribunal service continuity.

10. **Dependent claim — Tribunal-verdict-based proactive surface.** The method of claim 1 wherein prior-confirmed sweet reasoning-steps from persisted Synapses are proactively surfaced to new reasoning sessions by The Herald (#2282) when the new session begins reasoning about a similar problem, such that the reasoning agent begins with awareness of Tribunal-verified reasoning-patterns applicable to the domain, avoiding re-derivation of reasoning that has already been verified and catalogued.

11. **Dependent claim — three-bites-at-the-apple cross-vendor empirical instance.** The method of claim 1 wherein the anticipated first empirical instance comprises Knight (Sonnet 4.6) as primary reasoner, Bishop (Opus 4.7) as primary Critic, Pawn (Perplexity Sonar-Pro) as secondary Critic, enabling the cooperative substrate's self-verification to leverage three independent model families simultaneously at per-grape granularity, such that the Tribunal's quorum aggregates across model families with minimally-correlated error modes.

---

## Novelty anchor

No prior art combines: (i) reasoning-step-granularity (not output-level) verification, (ii) parallel multi-model Critic pool with structured verdicts, (iii) user-selectable granularity primitive analogous to 3D-printing layer-height selection, (iv) Stone-Tablet grounding discipline with summaries-excluded as structural requirement, (v) integration with append-only reasoning-cache substrate, (vi) cross-Cathedral Critic composition with scope-permissioning, (vii) cooperative-governance-mandated minimum verification depths for specific decision classes.

Adjacent art (mixture-of-experts, LLM ensembles, voting classifiers, reasoning-as-self-critique patterns in prompting literature, adversarial verification frameworks in ML safety research) each addresses subsets. None combine with the cooperative-substrate semantics, user-selectable granularity, and Stone-Tablet discipline.

---

## Why this is a Crown Jewel

- **Solves the Sonnet-to-Sonnet fog at execution time**, not just retrospectively (#2287 addresses retroactive; #2288 addresses real-time).
- **Makes reasoning verification user-selectable rather than engineer-embedded.** Operators choose verification depth per session based on stakes. Governance can mandate depths for decision classes.
- **Converts cross-vendor AI diversity into a reasoning-quality primitive.** Vendor-Agnostic Cathedral Effect (#2281 claim 3) generalizes to Vendor-Agnostic Reasoning Verification (different vendors catch different reasoning errors). Cross-vendor ensemble becomes architecturally structural, not accidental.
- **Stone-Tablet grounding is substrate-enforced.** Speculation cannot pass as argument. Summaries are excluded mechanically. Reasoning quality becomes auditable against immutable canon.
- **Integrates with every existing Stitchpunk class.** Doesn't require re-architecture of existing #2270-#2287; extends them with a new operational layer.

---

## Founder-voice anchors (B121)

- **"Critical Analysis"** — operational method name (Founder coinage)
- **"Sweet vs bitter grapes"** — grape-quality verdicts, extending #2287 taxonomy
- **"At LEAST two bites at the apple for a single AI"** — minimum self-verify discipline
- **"Two, three, or more AI that can simultaneously evaluate analysis on the fly and return thumbs up or down for each cluster, down to each GRAPE if we, as a user, chose the granular discrete method"** — the Tribunal mechanic, verbatim
- **"SLA not FDM — the accuracy and ability to have tiny .25 mm is IMPOSSIBLE for FDM, due to the nozzle size. So we can choose, as users, what level of marker we want"** — the user-selectable-granularity primitive, Founder's analogy
- **".2 analysis takes a little longer, but is rock solid accurate. 1.5 analysis is faster, but may not be as accurate, since it didn't have as many checks"** — canonical cost/accuracy trade-off framing
- **"Facts are derived from Stone Tablets or the equivalent — TRUTH, not maybes, and not summaries"** — grounding discipline verbatim

Run K472-class work through the Tribunal at SLA-Depth .5. Compare results against K472-baseline: does the Tribunal catch reasoning errors that K472 missed? Does it change outcome class? Does Founder detect subjective quality improvement in the resulting session artifacts?

## #2289 Cerberus (Retrospective Multi-Head Reasoning-Trace Examination)

## INNOVATION_THRESH — #2289 Cerberus: Retrospective Multi-Head Reasoning-Chain Examination

**Innovation:** #2289 — Cerberus: Retrospective Multi-Head Reasoning-Chain Examination with Iterative Head-Convergence and Root-Cause Trace-Back in a Cooperative Memory Substrate
**Bishop Session:** B121, 2026-04-24
**Author:** Bishop (Claude Opus 4.7, 1M context), Founder-proposed-and-ratified in-session
**Filing:** Prov 14 supplementary (per thresh-as-we-go mode; Founder extended window)
**Publication hold:** IN FORCE until Prov 14 receipt
**Related anchors:** #2269 Three Fates, #2270 Scribes Cathedral, #2278 Cathedral Effect, #2279 Hounds (Guard capability), #2280 Distributed-Function Coherence, #2281 Multi-Cathedral Substrate, #2283 Hound Guard Defense-in-Depth, #2287 Synapses, #2288 The Tribunal (Live Critical Analysis).

---

## TL;DR (2 lines)

**Cerberus is a multi-headed retrospective-examination Stitchpunk class (typically 2-3 AI "heads") that examines completed reasoning chains from multiple orthogonal angles simultaneously — result-first, grape-first, and pattern-first — converging iteratively on root-cause trace-backs.** Distinct in time-horizon from Hound Guard (transport-time) and The Tribunal (reasoning-time); Cerberus operates at retrospection-time, catching what live layers missed and surfacing reasoning that no longer applies to present conditions.

---

## The Problem

Live verification layers (Tribunal, Guard) cannot catch every failure class:

1. **Pattern-level failures only visible across chains.** A single reasoning-chain may look locally consistent but conflict with prior-chain patterns. Tribunal examines within-chain; doesn't cross-reference.
2. **Hindsight-only evidence.** Some reasoning defects are invisible until result appears. E.g., reasoning that "seemed reasonable" at each step produces a result that contradicts established canon. The contradiction is retrospective evidence for the defect.
3. **Stale-reasoning propagation (turkey-pan trap per #2287 claim 10).** Conditions change after reasoning was concluded; inherited practices based on prior-reasoning need retrospective re-examination when cited Stone Tablets change.
4. **Governance challenges require post-hoc reasoning audit.** When a cooperative member disputes a decision, the reasoning that produced the decision must be examined forensically — not in real-time (decision already happened) but thoroughly (the challenge is serious).
5. **Cross-tier retrospective critique.** Higher-capability models (Opus) should be able to retrospectively critique lower-tier (Sonnet) reasoning per #2287 claim 2, but need a structured examination protocol, not ad-hoc review.
6. **Regular audit discipline.** Cooperative governance benefits from rotating/random audits of landed reasoning to maintain substrate quality at scale.

**Existing solutions fail:**

- **Tribunal (#2288)** — real-time only; doesn't examine completed chains
- **Hound Guard (#2283)** — transport-layer only; doesn't examine reasoning
- **Traditional post-mortem processes** — human-operator-driven, not scalable, not substrate-integrated, not multi-perspective
- **Single-AI retrospective critique** — inherits single-model blind spots; Sonnet-to-Sonnet fog at retrospective layer too

The gap: a **multi-head, parallel-perspective, iterative-convergence retrospective examination substrate integrated with the cooperative reasoning record.**

---

## The Mechanism

### Cerberus as three-headed examination agent class

**Cerberus** comprises 2-3 AI "heads," each examining a completed reasoning chain (vine + clusters + grapes + result from #2287) from a distinct analytical angle:

- **Head 1 — Result-First:** Starts from the final result. Reasons backward through the chain: *"what upstream grape decisions produced this result? Trace the dependencies. Identify which grapes were load-bearing and which were not."* Produces a **backward dependency trace**.
- **Head 2 — Grape-First:** Examines each grape on its own merits, out-of-chain-context. *"Is this grape Stone-Tablet-grounded? Does the citation resolve to current canon? Is the reasoning step internally sound?"* Produces a **grape-by-grape quality inventory**.
- **Head 3 — Pattern-First:** Compares this vine to prior similar vines in the commons. *"Does this reasoning-chain match a known-good pattern? A known-failure pattern? A novel pattern?"* Produces a **pattern-recognition report** with cross-vine references.

### Iterative head-convergence

Heads operate in parallel initially, then iteratively share findings:

1. **Round 1:** each head produces its independent report
2. **Round 2:** heads cross-read each other's reports; each head re-examines its own analysis in light of other heads' findings (*"Head 2 flagged grape 14 as ungrounded, which aligns with my Head 1 finding that grape 14 is load-bearing for the anomalous result"*)
3. **Round 3+:** iterative convergence — heads agree on root-cause or explicitly surface disagreement
4. **Output:** structured Cerberus report — root-cause trace-back, contributing factors, recommended remediations, disagreement surface (if any)

Iterative convergence typically stabilizes in 2-3 rounds. A session tuning parameter controls max iterations.

### Cerberus vs Tribunal — clear distinctions

| Dimension | Tribunal (#2288) | Cerberus (#2289) |
|---|---|---|
| Time | Real-time (during reasoning) | Retrospective (after reasoning completes) |
| Scope | Per reasoning-step (grape) | Per reasoning-chain (vine) or per-cluster |
| Mechanic | Parallel verdicts, quorum aggregation | Multi-perspective examination, iterative convergence |
| Output | Grape-level verdicts (sweet/bitter/...) | Root-cause trace-back report |
| Use case | Prevent bad reasoning from chaining | Diagnose why reasoning produced specific outcomes |

Both layers integrate with #2287 Synapses. Neither substitutes for the other.

### Trigger conditions

Cerberus is invoked when one or more trigger conditions fire:

- **Outcome anomaly** — result violates pre-registered prediction or quality threshold
- **Stale-reasoning flag (per #2287 claim 10)** — a cited Stone Tablet changed; turkey-pan detector fires
- **Governance challenge** — cooperative member or operator disputes a decision
- **Audit sampling** — regular/random examination at configurable rate
- **Cross-tier retroactive request** — higher-capability-model examines lower-tier work
- **Cross-Cathedral examination request** — one member-Cathedral requests Cerberus on another's public-scope reasoning (with scope permission)

### Integration with existing Stitchpunk Corps

- **#2287 Synapses** — Cerberus inputs are Synapses; Cerberus reports are themselves Synapses (annotation-class). Every retrospective examination becomes part of the persisted reasoning record.
- **#2288 Tribunal** — if Tribunal missed a reasoning defect (e.g., chain was below SLA-Depth threshold), Cerberus catches it retrospectively. The layers reinforce.
- **#2283 Hound Guard** — Cerberus howls on anomalies detected; Guard pipeline applies.
- **#2284 Nurse** — Cerberus head-health monitored; failover to peer head if a head degrades (head-equivalent of Nurse's Scribe-peer-failover).
- **Scrambler A/B/C** — when heads cannot converge after iterative rounds, Scrambler arbitrates.
- **#2279 Hounds** — Cerberus reports transport cross-Cathedral via Atropos-Cerberus-Hounds (high-priority, adversarial-capable payload class).
- **#2282 Herald** — surfaces prior Cerberus reports to new sessions examining similar territory.
- **#2285 Catacombs + Alexandrian Library** — public-scope Cerberus reports surface as cooperative-learning material (studying expert retrospective analysis = onboarding accelerator).

### Head composition at scale

For cooperative LB:
- **Head 1 (Result-First):** Opus-class preferred (deep reasoning for backward tracing)
- **Head 2 (Grape-First):** Sonnet-class sufficient (citation-verification is well-structured)
- **Head 3 (Pattern-First):** cross-vendor preferred (Perplexity or Google Flash) for diversity — different model families catch different patterns

Three-head composition aligns with the three-bites-cross-vendor (Sonnet/Opus/Pawn) pattern of the Cathedral Effect #2281 claim 3, applied at the retrospective-examination layer.

---

## Claims (hypothesis scope)

1. **Independent claim (method).** A method for retrospective multi-perspective examination of completed AI-agent reasoning chains within a cooperative memory substrate, comprising:
   (a) receiving a completed reasoning chain comprising a hierarchical record of problem-space (vine), reasoning-clusters, and individual reasoning-steps (grapes) with associated final result;
   (b) dispatching the chain to a set of two or more AI "heads" (the Cerberus), each head configured to examine the chain from a distinct analytical perspective;
   (c) at minimum three examination perspectives comprising: result-first backward-dependency tracing, grape-first independent-quality inventory, and pattern-first cross-chain-comparison against prior reasoning in the substrate;
   (d) operating the heads first in parallel to produce independent reports, then iteratively in cross-reading rounds wherein each head re-examines its analysis in light of other heads' findings;
   (e) iterating cross-reading rounds until convergence (heads agree on root-cause) or until a maximum-iteration parameter is reached (surfacing explicit disagreement if unresolved);
   (f) producing a structured retrospective report comprising root-cause trace-back, contributing factors, recommended remediations, and explicit disagreement-surface if heads did not fully converge;
   (g) persisting the retrospective report as an annotation-synapse within the cooperative substrate, scope-permissioned, available for future-session surface.

2. **Dependent claim — trigger conditions.** The method of claim 1 wherein Cerberus invocation is triggered by one or more of: outcome anomaly exceeding pre-registered thresholds, stale-reasoning flag from citation-drift detection, cooperative-member governance-challenge, regular audit-sampling at configurable rate, cross-capability-tier retroactive critique request, or cross-cathedral examination request with appropriate scope permissions.

3. **Dependent claim — three-perspective composition.** The method of claim 1 wherein the minimum three perspectives of (c) are structurally distinguished: the result-first perspective operates via backward-traversal of decision dependencies starting from the chain's final result; the grape-first perspective operates via per-reasoning-step quality evaluation independent of chain context; the pattern-first perspective operates via cross-referencing the chain against a persisted corpus of prior reasoning chains for matching, divergent, or novel patterns.

4. **Dependent claim — cross-vendor head diversity.** The method of claim 1 wherein the heads comprise AI agents from at least two distinct vendor families selected to maximize uncorrelated error modes in retrospective examination, extending the Vendor-Agnostic property of the Cathedral Effect (#2281) to the retrospective-reasoning-verification layer.

5. **Dependent claim — higher-capability-tier head.** The method of claim 1 wherein at least one head operates at a capability tier equal to or higher than the agent that produced the reasoning chain being examined, enabling cross-tier retrospective critique per #2287 claim 2 while producing structured multi-perspective output rather than ad-hoc critique.

6. **Dependent claim — iterative head-convergence protocol.** The method of claim 1 wherein iterative cross-reading rounds are structured: each head produces an independent report in round 1; in subsequent rounds, each head receives all other heads' prior-round reports and may amend, expand, or concur with its own analysis; rounds continue until either all heads converge on a root-cause trace-back or a pre-configured maximum-iteration parameter triggers explicit-disagreement surface.

7. **Dependent claim — stale-reasoning turkey-pan trigger.** The method of claim 1 wherein when a cited Stone Tablet in a previously-completed reasoning chain subsequently changes (canonical value updated, environmental condition evolved), Cerberus is automatically invoked on the affected chain to examine whether the reasoning still holds under updated canon, preventing propagation of practices whose justifying conditions have lapsed (the turkey-pan detector of #2287 claim 10 operating at retrospective-examination-depth).

8. **Dependent claim — integration with Synapses substrate.** The method of claim 1 wherein the reasoning-chain input of (a) comprises Synapses records per #2287; the retrospective report of (f) is itself persisted as annotation-Synapses; and the complete Cerberus examination becomes part of the cooperative reasoning commons, scope-permissioned for study, teaching, and pattern-extraction by future reasoning agents.

9. **Dependent claim — integration with Tribunal (#2288).** The method of claim 1 wherein Cerberus's retrospective examination catches reasoning defects that escape live Tribunal verification (defects invisible until chain completes, defects only visible cross-chain, defects specific to pattern-recognition tasks), and wherein Tribunal-verdict data from the chain's live-verification history is input to Cerberus's examination, enabling Cerberus to analyze not just the reasoning but also the live-verification quality during chain production.

10. **Dependent claim — governance-audit workflow.** The method of claim 1 wherein a cooperative member dispute-filing against a governance decision triggers Cerberus examination of the decision's reasoning chain as a structured forensic audit, with the Cerberus report becoming admissible evidence in the cooperative's dispute-resolution process, and wherein Structural Bylaw changes require accompanying Cerberus examination to demonstrate the change is grounded in re-examined canon rather than turkey-pan inheritance.

11. **Dependent claim — audit-sampling protocol.** The method of claim 1 wherein cooperative-substrate governance defines a configurable audit-sampling rate (e.g., 1-in-N vines, rotating per category, risk-weighted by decision-class), triggering Cerberus examination on sampled chains regardless of whether they show anomaly, maintaining substrate-wide reasoning-quality discipline as a continuous process rather than event-driven response.

---

## Novelty anchor

No prior art combines: (i) retrospective examination of reasoning chains (not just outputs), (ii) multi-head parallel architecture with three distinct analytical perspectives (result-first, grape-first, pattern-first), (iii) iterative head-convergence protocol producing structured disagreement-surface, (iv) integration with append-only reasoning-cache substrate, (v) trigger-condition taxonomy spanning anomaly-detection, stale-reasoning, governance-challenge, audit-sampling, and cross-tier critique, (vi) cross-vendor head composition for uncorrelated-error-mode diversity, (vii) cooperative-governance integration (audit-sampling protocol, dispute-resolution workflow, bylaw-change-grounding requirement).

Adjacent art (post-mortem analysis frameworks, debugging tools, LLM-as-judge patterns, multi-agent debate frameworks, reasoning-chain audit papers) each addresses subsets without the cooperative-substrate-native semantics, multi-perspective discipline, iterative-convergence protocol, or governance-workflow integration.

---

## Why this is a Crown Jewel

- **Completes the three-layer defense stack.** Guard (transport-time) + Tribunal (reasoning-time) + Cerberus (retrospection-time) = complete temporal coverage of reasoning-quality substrate defense.
- **Operationalizes the turkey-pan detector.** Claim 7 automates stale-reasoning examination when cited canon changes. Inherited practices get re-examined without operator intervention.
- **Makes governance dispute-resolution structural.** Claim 10 provides a Cerberus-generated audit-report pattern that cooperative members can rely on for dispute-filings, giving the governance layer a reasoning-examination primitive rather than operator judgment.
- **Preserves cross-vendor AI diversity at the retrospective layer.** Three-head cross-vendor composition extends the Vendor-Agnostic Cathedral Effect finding (K455a / #2281 claim 3) into retrospective verification.
- **Creates a retrospective-reasoning-commons via Herald surfacing.** Expert retrospective examinations become teaching material. New members can study not just how-to-reason but how-to-examine-reasoning.

---

## Founder-voice anchors (B121)

- **"Cerberus"** — the three-headed dog of Greek mythology, Founder's chosen naming (mythological coherence with Hounds, Fates, Scribes, Nurse, Herald, Tribunal, etc.)
- **"Reason backwards, at a more iterative level"** — the method described verbatim
- **Implicit: the underworld-guardian metaphor.** Cerberus in mythology prevents dead from leaving, living from entering. In LB: prevents stale reasoning from propagating forward into active substrate, prevents intrusion/corruption of preserved reasoning records.

---

## First empirical instance (anticipated)

K600+ implementation session (post-Tribunal MVP K500-504). Minimal Cerberus instantiation: Bishop (Opus) as Head 1, Knight (Sonnet) as Head 2, optionally Pawn (Perplexity API) as Head 3. First examination target: retrospective analysis of K455a's 14pp ceiling-bounded Cathedral Effect result — did Cerberus catch retrieval-layer issues that K455c/K455a live benchmarks missed? If yes, first reduction-to-practice for #2289 claims 1-11.

- **Expected 102/103 art:** LLM-as-judge patterns, multi-agent debate frameworks, post-mortem/root-cause-analysis tools, adversarial verification in ML safety. None combine with cooperative-substrate-native integration, three-perspective structural discipline, iterative convergence protocol, and governance-workflow integration.

## #2290 The Loom (Domain-Scribe Active Participation in Reasoning Production)

## INNOVATION_THRESH — #2290 The Loom: Active Domain-Scribe Participation in Reasoning Production

**Innovation:** #2290 — The Loom: Active Domain-Scribe Participation in Reasoning Production with Per-Grape Multi-Domain Expertise Injection in a Cooperative Memory Substrate
**Bishop Session:** B121, 2026-04-24
**Author:** Bishop (Claude Opus 4.7, 1M context), Founder-proposed-and-ratified in-session
**Filing:** Prov 14 supplementary (thresh-as-we-go)
**Publication hold:** IN FORCE until Prov 14 receipt
**Related anchors:** #2269 Three Fates, #2270 Scribes Cathedral, #2276 Scribe Coverage Discovery, #2278 Cathedral Effect, #2281 Multi-Cathedral Substrate, #2282 Herald, #2287 Synapses, #2288 The Tribunal, #2289 Cerberus.

---

## TL;DR (2 lines)

**The Loom is a new Stitchpunk class that routes each reasoning-step (grape, per #2287) to domain-expertise-Scribes whose declared expertise matches the grape's subject, and ingests their domain-specific contributions INTO the reasoning-production process — not as surfaced content (Herald's role) and not as general verification (Tribunal's role), but as active domain-expertise injection that shapes the next grape.** Completes the architectural landing of the "weaving" concept Founder deferred from B120: Fates spin threads, Scribes contribute domain-threads, the Loom weaves them into reasoning fabric as it's produced.

---

## The Problem

Domain expertise in current AI-agent architectures is delivered either:

1. **Passively** (RAG, Herald-style surfacing per #2282): relevant content is surfaced based on keyword/semantic match; the reasoner decides whether and how to use it. Expertise is a reference, not a voice at the table.
2. **Generically** (Tribunal-style live-verification per #2288): general-capability Critics evaluate reasoning-quality; domain-specialty is accidental if the Critic happens to have it, not structurally guaranteed.
3. **Post-hoc** (domain-expert review after production): the reasoning produces an artifact; an expert reviews it; corrections happen retroactively at production cost.

None of these deliver **active domain-expertise injection into the reasoning-production process itself** — domain Scribes acting not as content-surfacers but as structural participants whose declared expertise becomes part of the reasoning as it's being produced.

**Founder's laundry metaphor B121:** *"We wash the clothes as they are being made instead of after we are wearing them — we apply the scribes to the PROCESS of reasoning."* The current pattern cleans clothes after wearing; the Loom pattern cleans the fibers as they're being woven. Domain quality baked in at production time, not post-production repair.

**Existing solutions fail:**

- **RAG and vector retrieval** (Pinecone, Weaviate): deliver document chunks; don't deliver expertise as a voice
- **Herald proactive surfacing (#2282)**: surfaces Scribe content; doesn't structurally inject Scribe expertise into reasoning production
- **Tribunal live-verification (#2288)**: generalist Critics; domain specialty is accidental
- **Vendor-native custom GPTs / Projects / Spaces**: single-vendor, static, pre-session; not cooperative-substrate-integrated; not per-grape-granular
- **Multi-agent expert panels in research literature**: ad-hoc, not structured as persistent cooperative substrate, not integrated with immutable-fact grounding, not cross-Cathedral

The gap: **a cooperative-substrate-native mechanism for domain-Scribe-specialists to actively participate in per-grape reasoning-production**, with structured domain-expertise injection, per-Scribe-configurable granularity, and integration with the full Stitchpunk Corps.

---

## The Mechanism

### The Loom as Stitchpunk class

**The Loom** is a new Stitchpunk class that routes each reasoning-grape through a **per-grape Scribe panel** — the set of domain-Scribes whose declared expertise matches the grape's subject. Each domain-Scribe in the panel returns not a verdict (Tribunal's role) but a **domain-contribution**: specific expertise relevant to this grape, formatted as structured injection to shape the next reasoning-step.

For each grape produced:

1. **Domain-match routing:** the Loom identifies which Scribes' declared expertise matches the grape's subject. Uses existing Fates' Clotho classifier (#2269) extended with domain-selection for reasoning-time participation.
2. **Per-panel composition:** assembled set of domain-Scribes (could be 1 to many per grape, depending on how many domains the grape touches)
3. **Expertise injection:** each domain-Scribe in the panel contributes structured guidance: canonical values relevant to this grape, domain-bylaws that constrain it, prior-reasoning patterns in the domain, governance requirements that apply
4. **Structured input to next grape:** contributions feed into the reasoning agent's next reasoning-step, becoming part of the fabric — not a reference the reasoner consults, but an expertise-thread the reasoner weaves into the next grape
5. **Panel-output as Synapses:** domain-contributions themselves become Synapses (annotation-class per #2287), attributed to the contributing Scribe, persisted as part of the reasoning record

### The weaving metaphor (Founder's mythological coherence, landed B121)

Founder's metaphor chain across Stitchpunk Corps:

- **Scribes** record tablets
- **Fates** spin / measure / cut threads of destiny (textile mythology: Clotho the spinner, Lachesis the measurer, Atropos the cutter)
- **Hounds** transport
- **Herald** announces
- **Nurse** cares
- **Tribunal** verifies
- **Cerberus** examines retrospectively
- **The Loom** (this innovation) — weaves domain-threads into reasoning fabric

Founder B120 foresight: *"Harmony makes me think and sense a weaving... I'll address it next session."* That weaving concept **lands at B121 as The Loom**. Resonance (same-moment multiple voices) + Weaving (cross-domain orthogonal threads) = complete architectural coverage of multi-Scribe cooperative reasoning.

### Clear distinctions from existing layers

| Layer | Role | When | Mechanism |
|---|---|---|---|
| **Herald (#2282)** | Content-surface (passive) | Real-time | Watchlist match → surface tablets to reasoner |
| **Tribunal (#2288)** | Quality-verification (active) | Real-time | Parallel Critics cast verdicts on grapes |
| **Cerberus (#2289)** | Retrospective examination | Post-completion | Multi-head backward analysis of completed chains |
| **The Loom (#2290)** | **Domain-expertise injection (active)** | Real-time | Domain-Scribes contribute expertise-threads per grape |

All four operate on #2287 Synapses substrate. All four integrate with Hounds / Guard / Nurse. Together they cover the four temporal + modal quadrants of reasoning-substrate operation: passive/active × real-time/post-hoc.

### Per-Scribe granularity configuration

Different Scribes warrant different participation granularity based on their domain's stakes and per-session operator choice:

- **Governance-sensitive Scribes** (Harper Guild ethics-expertise, Structural Bylaws canon): MAY mandate participation on every grape touching their domain
- **Canonical-facts Scribes** (R11 corpus, canonical_values.yaml-Scribe): always-participate on any grape making factual claims matching their canon
- **Pattern-recognition Scribes** (KnightArchitecture, Decisions, Founder Voice): per-Scribe-configurable participation threshold; may be session-adjustable
- **Reference corpora Scribes** (mode: corpus per K466): participate when queries match the corpus; respect corpus-mode retrieval semantics

The per-Scribe configuration is analogous to SLA-Depth (#2288) but at the domain-Scribe layer — operators choose **which Scribes must weave into which grapes** as a cooperative-governance primitive.

### Integration with existing Stitchpunk Corps

- **#2287 Synapses** — Loom contributions are Synapses (domain-contribution annotation-class)
- **#2288 Tribunal** — Tribunal evaluates GENERAL quality; Loom injects DOMAIN expertise. Complementary. A grape may receive both a Tribunal verdict and a Loom panel's domain-contributions. They do not conflict.
- **#2289 Cerberus** — post-hoc Cerberus examination evaluates whether Loom contributions were correctly woven into the reasoning. Quality audit for Loom's output-integration.
- **#2269 Three Fates** — Clotho's classifier extended: identifies both (a) which Scribe should receive the tablet for storage (existing role), and (b) which Scribes should be invited to the Loom panel for this grape (new role).
- **#2276 Scribe Coverage Discovery** — Loom surfaces per-domain participation; coverage gaps become visible at reasoning-production time, not just post-hoc. Drives Scribe-creation priorities.
- **#2279 Hounds** — Loom panels can span cross-Cathedral domain-Scribes: a grape touching Harper Guild expertise can invoke Harper-scoped Scribes from multiple member-Cathedrals, transported via Lachesis-Hounds (scorer-class, since the Loom is a scoring-weighted participation primitive).
- **#2281 Multi-Cathedral Substrate** — Loom composition can draw from any member-Cathedral with appropriate scope permission, creating cross-member expertise-pooling for a single reasoning session.
- **#2282 Herald** — Herald surfaces content; the Loom leverages Herald's detection to identify panel members (Herald says "this content is relevant"; Loom says "and this Scribe should participate").
- **#2285 Catacombs + Alexandrian Library** — dormant Scribes can be called-forth into Loom panels on governance-mandated triggers (e.g., a bylaw-adjacent reasoning-step triggers call-forth of dormant bylaw-history Scribes).

---

## Claims (hypothesis scope)

1. **Independent claim (method).** A method for active domain-expertise injection into AI-agent reasoning production within a cooperative memory substrate, comprising:
   (a) receiving a reasoning-step produced by a primary AI agent, the reasoning-step structured per an append-only reasoning-cache protocol comprising agent identifier, timestamp, reasoning-content, and cited facts;
   (b) identifying a panel of domain-specialist Scribes whose declared expertise-domains match the reasoning-step's subject, via classifier agent examining the reasoning-step content and declared Scribe-domain registries;
   (c) for each domain-Scribe in the panel, generating a structured domain-contribution comprising at minimum: canonical values from the Scribe's domain relevant to the reasoning-step, applicable domain-governance constraints, relevant prior-reasoning patterns, and any substrate-level cautions;
   (d) injecting the domain-contributions into the primary agent's reasoning-production context prior to production of the next reasoning-step, such that the domain expertise becomes part of the reasoning fabric rather than a reference consulted after-the-fact;
   (e) persisting each domain-contribution as an annotation-cache entry in the cooperative substrate, attributed to the contributing Scribe, enabling downstream examination, teaching, and substrate-quality measurement;
   (f) enforcing scope permissioning: a domain-Scribe's contribution is available to the reasoning-step only if the Scribe's scope (public, guild-named, tribe-named, project-named, or private per prior substrate innovations) is accessible to the reasoning-agent's member-identity;
   (g) operating concurrently with other substrate layers (content-surface, general-verification, retrospective-examination) without conflicting role-assignment: domain-Scribes contribute expertise, not verdicts; contribution does not substitute for verification.

2. **Dependent claim — Fates-routed panel assembly.** The method of claim 1 wherein the classifier of (b) is the substrate's Clotho (classifier-Fate per #2269), extended to produce dual output: tablet-routing destination AND Loom-panel composition, such that the same classifier infrastructure serves both content-placement and expertise-participation routing.

3. **Dependent claim — per-Scribe participation thresholds.** The method of claim 1 wherein each domain-Scribe declares a participation-threshold governing when it contributes to Loom panels: governance-sensitive Scribes mandate participation on all grapes touching their domain; canonical-facts Scribes participate on any factual claim matching their canon; pattern-recognition Scribes participate based on configurable cooperative-operator settings.

4. **Dependent claim — cross-Cathedral Loom panels.** The method of claim 1 wherein Loom panels may include domain-Scribes from cooperative-member-Cathedrals other than the one in which the reasoning is being produced, subject to scope permissions and cross-Cathedral transport via appropriate Hounds, enabling cross-member expertise pooling within single reasoning sessions.

5. **Dependent claim — governance-mandated participation.** The method of claim 1 wherein cooperative-substrate governance may mandate Loom-panel composition for specific decision-classes: Structural Bylaw decisions mandate participation of the Structural Bylaws Scribe; Harper Guild ethics cases mandate participation of all Harper-Scoped Scribes; patent-filing-adjacent decisions mandate participation of the IP Ledger Scribes and prior-art Scribes.

6. **Dependent claim — weaving-metaphor-coherent output structure.** The method of claim 1 wherein domain-contributions from multiple Scribes are woven into the reasoning-step's output context as distinguishable threads with explicit attribution (e.g., "Harper contributes:...", "Architecture contributes:...", "Founder-Voice contributes:..."), such that the reasoning agent can distinguish expertise-sources and weigh them appropriately rather than receiving an undifferentiated merged context.

7. **Dependent claim — complementary to Tribunal verification.** The method of claim 1 wherein the method operates concurrently with but distinctly from general-quality-verification (Tribunal per #2288): the Loom's output is domain-expertise-contribution shaping the next grape; the Tribunal's output is quality-verdict on the current grape; these operations occur in parallel without role-conflict, producing complementary improvements to reasoning-quality.

8. **Dependent claim — dormant-Scribe call-forth on Loom trigger.** The method of claim 1 wherein a dormant Scribe (Catacombs-resident per #2285) may be called-forth into a Loom panel by governance trigger — for example, a bylaw-adjacent reasoning-step triggers call-forth of bylaw-history Scribes preserving conditions-under-which-bylaws-were-adopted, enabling turkey-pan-trap detection at reasoning-production time rather than post-hoc.

9. **Dependent claim — Scribe Coverage Discovery extension.** The method of claim 1 wherein Loom panel compositions over time are aggregated per-domain to surface coverage gaps at reasoning-production time (extending Scribe Coverage Discovery per #2276), such that cooperative members observe which domains are under-represented in active reasoning participation and are guided to contribute Scribes in those domains.

10. **Dependent claim — contribution-quality recursion.** The method of claim 1 wherein domain-contributions themselves become subject to Tribunal live-verification: a Scribe's contribution to a grape is verified by Tribunal Critics before injection, preventing low-quality domain-contributions from polluting reasoning fabric; Scribes accumulate contribution-quality reputation analogous to vouch-credit per #2284 Scribe Mutual Aid Protocol.

11. **Dependent claim — weaving-concept reduction-to-practice.** The method of claim 1 is the first empirical reduction-to-practice of the "weaving" architectural concept foreshadowed in Founder session B120, materially distinct from the "resonance" concept (same-moment multiple voices reinforcing) embodied in prior innovations #2270 Scribes Cathedral and #2278 Cathedral Effect. Resonance + Weaving = complete architectural-metaphor coverage of multi-Scribe cooperative reasoning participation.

---

## Novelty anchor

No prior art combines: (i) active domain-Scribe participation in reasoning-production (not passive surfacing, not general verification), (ii) per-grape panel assembly via classifier-routed Scribe selection, (iii) structured attributed expertise-contribution format, (iv) integration with append-only reasoning-cache substrate, (v) governance-mandated Loom composition for decision-classes, (vi) cross-Cathedral panel composition, (vii) coherent mythological-coordinate integration with complete Stitchpunk Corps at four time/mode quadrants (Herald / Tribunal / Cerberus / Loom).

Adjacent art: RAG systems (retrieve content, don't inject expertise), multi-agent systems (task decomposition, not per-grape expertise), vendor-native project memory (static pre-session, not per-grape active), academic multi-expert frameworks (ad-hoc, not substrate-native). None combine with cooperative-governance + scope-permissioning + mythological-coordinate architecture.

---

## Why this is a Crown Jewel

- **Completes the four-layer reasoning-substrate architecture.** Herald (passive-surface) + Tribunal (active-verification) + Cerberus (retrospective-examination) + **Loom (active-injection)** = complete coverage.
- **Lands the B120 weaving concept architecturally.** Founder foresight at B120 becomes Founder-proposed architecture at B121. Proves the metaphor-chain is not decorative — it's predictive of substrate needs.
- **Makes cooperative expertise first-class in reasoning production.** Members' domain-Scribes are not references; they're voices at the table. This is the cooperative-substrate's answer to the siloed-expert-system pattern.
- **Extends Cathedral Effect cooperative-corpus flywheel to expertise-injection layer.** More Scribes = more domains-available-to-weave = more expertise-threads in every reasoning session = higher-quality reasoning. Measurable via #2276 Scribe Coverage Discovery extended.
- **Preserves cooperative-governance discipline.** Governance can mandate Scribe participation on decision-classes; turkey-pan detection operates at reasoning-production time, not just post-hoc.

---

## Founder-voice anchors (B121)

- **"We apply the scribes to the PROCESS of reasoning"** — Loom's purpose-statement verbatim
- **"Wash the clothes as they are being made instead of after we are wearing them"** — Loom's canonical metaphor; contrast between production-time and post-production repair
- **"What each of the Scribe types do - can be done on a granular level here"** — Founder insight that Scribe-type expertise extends to reasoning-step granularity
- **"(And we will STILL do that)"** — explicit preservation of the existing Herald prompt-discussion pattern; Loom ADDS, doesn't replace
- **The B120 weaving foresight** (verbatim memory): *"Harmony makes me think and sense a weaving... I'll address it next session."* — fulfilled B121 via The Loom

---

## First empirical instance (anticipated)

K700+ implementation session (post-Tribunal MVP K500-504 and post-Cerberus MVP K600). Minimal Loom instantiation: Clotho-classifier extension to produce dual output (tablet-routing + Loom-panel); structured domain-contribution format; integration with one canonical Scribe (e.g., Canonical Values Scribe) as first Loom participant. Test case: a reasoning-step making factual claim that touches canonical-values domain auto-invites the Canonical Values Scribe to contribute (via Loom) before next grape production. Observe: does reasoning-quality measurably improve compared to Herald-surface-only baseline?

---

None combine with cooperative-substrate-native integration, per-grape granularity, governance-mandated participation, or mythological-coordinate architecture with complete Stitchpunk-class distinctness.
